摘要：大規模的非結構化多模態數據流遭受高「數據熵」的困擾，妨礙了高效的人類知識獲取和高品質的AI後訓練。現有的被動標註範式，過度依賴啟發式規則或通用的VLM，成本高昂、單調乏味，且未能解鎖原始數據中深層的程序邏輯。我們將數據處理提升為一種可學習的能力，提出一種向代理數據定制的範式轉變，主動地精煉和結構化數據，以符合多樣化的用戶和下游意圖。為了克服訓練此類高階能力中的數據稀缺瓶頸，我們設計了一個兩階段的管道，將生成語義合成基於確定性的事實錨點，產生一個涵蓋五個核心物理和數字領域的大規模數據集。在此基礎上，$\text{DataClaw}_0$-9B模型將監督微調（SFT）與群體相對政策優化（GRPO）協同，實現與複雜精煉和定制意圖的強健對齊。為了系統地量化這一能力，我們構建了$\text{DataClaw}_0$-val，這是首個專門針對數據精煉的基準。關鍵是，我們將下游後訓練作為最終的驗證基準。在視頻生成、現實世界VQA和GUI導航的評估中，確認$\text{DataClaw}_0$提供高信息密度的定制數據，促進模型在有限訓練數據環境下對新任務的高效適應。項目頁面：https://czjdsg.github.io/MakeAnyData

##### **Topological Neural Dynamics: A Neuron-wise Framework for Sequence Modeling**
2606.21295v1 by Borui Cai, Yao Zhao

Existing sequence models, including RNNs, LSTMs, continuous-time networks, and Transformers, share a common structural principle: layer-wise dynamics, where all neurons in the same layer co-evolve through a shared parameterized operator, leaving individual neurons no freedom to evolve independently. Yet in many complex dynamical systems, rich global behavior emerges precisely from locally evolving units interacting through structured connectivity. Inspired by this principle, we introduce Topological Neural Dynamics (TND), a sequence modeling framework that shifts computation from layer-wise to neuron-wise dynamics. TND represents a neural system as a directed neuron graph, an interaction operator, and a local dynamics function, where each neuron evolves independently and collective computation emerges from interactions through the explicit graph topology. We instantiate TND as a discrete-time graph-coupled dynamical system and evaluate it as a case study on a behavior cloning task in single-player Pong. Compared with Vanilla RNN, Sparse RNN, LSTM, Closed-form continuous-time neural network (CfC), and Transformer baselines, TND achieves the best catch rate and a mean of 17.47 consecutive catches per round, more than three times that of the strongest baseline. These results suggest that shifting from layer-wise to neuron-wise dynamics provides an effective inductive bias for sequence modeling.

摘要：現有的序列模型，包括RNN、LSTM、連續時間網絡和Transformer，具有共同的結構原則：層級動態，其中同一層的所有神經元通過共享的參數化運算子共同演化，使得個別神經元無法獨立演化。然而，在許多複雜的動態系統中，豐富的全局行為恰恰是由局部演化單元通過結構化連接互動而產生的。受到這一原則的啟發，我們引入了拓撲神經動態（TND），這是一種將計算從層級動態轉變為神經元動態的序列建模框架。TND將神經系統表示為一個有向神經元圖、一個互動運算子和一個局部動態函數，其中每個神經元獨立演化，集體計算則通過明確的圖拓撲中的互動而產生。我們將TND實現為一個離散時間圖耦合動態系統，並在單人Pong的行為複製任務中進行案例研究評估。與Vanilla RNN、Sparse RNN、LSTM、封閉形式連續時間神經網絡（CfC）和Transformer基線相比，TND達到了最佳的捕獲率，每輪平均17.47次連續捕獲，超過最強基線的三倍以上。這些結果表明，從層級動態轉變為神經元動態為序列建模提供了一種有效的歸納偏差。

##### **Beyond Hooking Onto the World: Referential Profiles and the Numerical Structure of LLM Grounding**
2606.21195v1 by Joo Yull Rhee

This paper revisits the grounding problem for large language models in light of recent vector-grounding accounts. I accept the shift from classical symbol grounding to vector grounding, but argue that the current debate remains incomplete in two respects. First, reference is often treated too thinly, as if it were a fixed link between an isolated expression and an object. I argue instead that reference is profile-based, context-sensitive, discourse-level, affectively shaped, and norm-governed. Even in the human case, reference is publicly stabilized through patterns of use, correction, distinction, inference, and continuation rather than through identical private representations. Second, vector grounding requires an account of numerical realization. LLMs do not acquire reference through human perception, memory, intention, embodiment, or understanding. Rather, through optimization, they parameterize linguistic traces of human world-directed practice. In a finite vector system, referential profiles must be distributed, may be superposed, and are recovered through context-sensitive computation. Weights, activations, attention-mediated hidden states, softmax-trained contrasts, and inner-product alignments are the mathematical sites at which inherited linguistic relations become stable and causally active. Mechanistic interpretability findings, including entity-like features, knowledge neurons, and emotion-related activation directions, provide indirect support for this view. They do not show that LLMs possess human reference. They support a more limited thesis: LLMs may possess derivative, language-mediated, profile-based, and numerically structured forms of reference.

摘要：這篇論文重新檢視了大型語言模型的基礎問題，考慮到最近的向量基礎說法。<lb/>我接受從傳統符號基礎轉向向量基礎的變化，但我認為當前的辯論在兩個方面仍然不完整。<lb/>首先，參考通常被過於簡化地對待，就好像它是孤立表達與對象之間的固定連結。<lb/>我則主張參考是基於輪廓的、上下文敏感的、話語層面的、情感塑造的，並且受到規範約束。<lb/>即使在人的情況下，參考也是通過使用、修正、區分、推理和延續的模式來公開穩定，而不是通過相同的私人表徵。<lb/>其次，向量基礎需要對數字實現的解釋。<lb/>大型語言模型並不是通過人類的感知、記憶、意圖、具身性或理解來獲得參考。<lb/>相反，通過優化，它們對人類面向世界的實踐的語言痕跡進行參數化。<lb/>在有限的向量系統中，參考輪廓必須是分佈的，可以是重疊的，並且通過上下文敏感的計算來恢復。<lb/>權重、激活、注意力介導的隱藏狀態、softmax訓練的對比以及內積對齊是遺傳語言關係變得穩定和因果活躍的數學場域。<lb/>機械可解釋性研究結果，包括類似實體的特徵、知識神經元和情感相關的激活方向，為這一觀點提供了間接支持。<lb/>它們並未顯示大型語言模型擁有人類參考。<lb/>它們支持一個更有限的論點：大型語言模型可能擁有衍生的、語言介導的、基於輪廓的和數字結構化的參考形式。

##### **Context-Aware Generative AI for Automated Telecom Test Script Generation**
2606.21151v1 by Gautam Prasad, Chandramohan T. N., Joy Bose

Automated test generation for telecom software systems and networks has advanced significantly with the adoption of machine learning and rule-based approaches. However, most existing solutions generate static test suites against a snapshot of the system; as code, configurations, topologies, and key performance indicators (KPIs) evolve, these tests quickly become outdated or misaligned with the live system. There is currently no widely adopted solution that continuously detects fine-grained changes and selectively adapts only the affected tests without regenerating entire test suites. This paper presents a context-aware generative AI framework for automated telecom test script generation that treats testing as a continuously adapting process driven by the current state of the system rather than a static artifact. The central contribution is delta-conditioned test generation over a live knowledge graph: our approach employs a continuously updated knowledge graph (KG) as a single source of truth, a delta engine for fine-grained change detection, and a KG-guided generative AI agent, operating via the Model Context Protocol (MCP), to create, update, or retire test cases automatically. We further integrate Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) to enrich reasoning with telecom-domain knowledge and historical artifacts. We demonstrate applicability across software-system and telecom-network use cases, including a Python-based KPI monitoring application managed in GitLab, and show how the framework reduces manual effort, improves test relevance, and accelerates test cycles.

摘要：自動化測試生成在電信軟體系統和網路方面隨著機器學習和基於規則的方法的採用而顯著進步。<lb/>然而，大多數現有解決方案是針對系統快照生成靜態測試套件；隨著代碼、配置、拓撲和關鍵績效指標（KPI）的演變，這些測試很快就會過時或與實時系統不匹配。<lb/>目前尚無廣泛採用的解決方案能夠持續檢測細粒度變更，並僅選擇性地調整受影響的測試，而無需重新生成整個測試套件。<lb/>本文提出了一個上下文感知的生成式人工智慧框架，用於自動化電信測試腳本生成，將測試視為一個根據系統當前狀態持續適應的過程，而非靜態的產物。<lb/>其核心貢獻是基於實時知識圖的增量條件測試生成：我們的方法使用不斷更新的知識圖（KG）作為唯一的真實來源，並利用增量引擎進行細粒度變更檢測，以及通過模型上下文協議（MCP）運作的KG引導生成式AI代理，自動創建、更新或退役測試案例。<lb/>我們進一步整合檢索增強生成（RAG），以豐富電信領域知識和歷史文物的推理。<lb/>我們展示了該框架在軟體系統和電信網路用例中的適用性，包括在GitLab中管理的基於Python的KPI監控應用程式，並展示了該框架如何減少手動工作、提高測試相關性並加快測試週期。

##### **PulseCX: Breaking the Closed-World Assumption in Real-Time CX**
2606.21124v1 by Rajat Agarwal, Suvidha Tripathi, Shubham Sharma

Conversational AI agents in Customer Experience (CX) typically suffer from a Closed-World Constraint, ignoring high-velocity external shifts like viral trends or outages. Ad-hoc web search attempts to bridge this gap but often introduce prohibitive latency and context poisoning. We introduce PulseCX, a framework that decouples knowledge acquisition from consumption. Adopting a structure-first paradigm, PulseCX employs an asynchronous agent to linearize signals into a Decay-Aware Temporal Knowledge Graph (DA-TKG) governed by reinforcement--decay dynamics to actively manage information lifecycles. By coupling this self-evolving memory with hierarchical intent gating, PulseCX removes synchronous search bottlenecks (<10ms overhead) and drives significant gains in Intent Resolution (IRR) and Customer Satisfaction (s-CSAT) in dynamic environments.

摘要：對話式人工智慧代理在客戶體驗 (CX) 中通常受到封閉世界限制的影響，忽略了像病毒趨勢或故障這樣的高速度外部變化。臨時的網路搜尋試圖彌補這一差距，但往往會引入過高的延遲和上下文污染。我們介紹了 PulseCX，一個將知識獲取與消費解耦的框架。採用結構優先的範式，PulseCX 使用異步代理將信號線性化為一個受強化-衰減動力學驅動的衰減感知時間知識圖 (DA-TKG)，以主動管理信息生命周期。通過將這種自我演化的記憶與分層意圖閘結合，PulseCX 消除了同步搜尋瓶頸（<10ms 的開銷），並在動態環境中驅動意圖解析 (IRR) 和客戶滿意度 (s-CSAT) 的顯著提升。

##### **A Multi-Agent Audit Framework for High-Stakes Reasoning: Evaluation and Interpretability in Clinical Mental Health Screening**
2606.21123v1 by Jingchen Ye, Yanpei Yu, Luyao Zhang

High-stakes reasoning tasks necessitate transparent and verifiable workflows, yet conventional single-model large language models (LLMs) often struggle with hallucination and low interpretability under zero-shot paradigms. To address this general AI challenge, we propose a Multi-Agent Audit Framework that simulates a collaborative, multi-step verification process. We empirically validate this architecture in the sensitive domain of clinical mental health screening using a modular LangChain workflow. Our framework decomposes the reasoning process into a Perception Agent, Knowledge Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), Chain-of-Thought (CoT) clinical inference, and a critical Audit verification stage. We evaluated this framework on the DAIC-WOZ dataset using locally deployed open-source models. Experimental results demonstrate that our multi-agent pipeline significantly outperforms single-agent baselines, reducing the Mean Absolute Error (MAE) for PHQ-8 depression severity prediction from 5.35 to 5.02. By exposing cross-agent validation traces, the framework mitigates reasoning drift and provides highly interpretable diagnostic rationales, offering a generalizable paradigm for reliable AI-assisted decision support beyond isolated model scaling. We make data and code open access on GitHub for replicability.

摘要：高風險推理任務需要透明且可驗證的工作流程，然而傳統的單模型大型語言模型（LLMs）在零樣本範式下常常面臨幻覺和低可解釋性的挑戰。為了解決這一普遍的人工智慧挑戰，我們提出了一個多代理審核框架，模擬協作的多步驗證過程。我們在臨床心理健康篩查這一敏感領域中，使用模塊化的LangChain工作流程對該架構進行了實證驗證。我們的框架將推理過程分解為感知代理、知識檢索增強生成（RAG）、思維鏈（CoT）臨床推理和關鍵的審核驗證階段。我們在DAIC-WOZ數據集上使用本地部署的開源模型對該框架進行了評估。實驗結果顯示，我們的多代理管道顯著優於單代理基準，將PHQ-8抑鬱嚴重性預測的平均絕對誤差（MAE）從5.35降低到5.02。通過暴露跨代理驗證痕跡，該框架減輕了推理漂移並提供了高度可解釋的診斷理由，為可靠的AI輔助決策支持提供了一個可泛化的範式，超越了孤立模型的擴展。我們在GitHub上開放數據和代碼以便於重複實驗。

##### **SLeDGe: Semi-Supervised Learning on Data Streams with Graph Structure Learning**
2606.21096v1 by Heechan Moon, Kijung Shin

Semi-supervised learning (SSL) on data streams is challenging due to the continuous evolution of high-volume data and the scarcity of labels. Existing methods are limited in leveraging the intrinsic relationships among samples because they typically rely on fixed similarity measures or static graph structures, which cannot capture how relationships evolve over time. We propose SLeDGe, an SSL method for data streams that jointly learns a predictive model and an adaptive graph structure under strict memory and label constraints. SLeDGe maintains compact labeled and unlabeled memories using distinct update strategies, balancing rapid adaptation to novel features with the retention of historical consistency. In addition, by encouraging sparsity in the relational graph, SLeDGe filters out spurious connections and enables effective propagation of label supervision. Across 12 datasets, SLeDGe outperforms state-of-the-art competitors, achieving average relative accuracy gains of 31.7% with 0.1% labels and 14.8% with 1% labels.

摘要：半監督學習（SSL）在數據流上的應用面臨挑戰，因為高容量數據的持續演變和標籤的稀缺。現有的方法在利用樣本之間的內在關係方面受到限制，因為它們通常依賴於固定的相似性度量或靜態圖結構，這無法捕捉關係隨時間的演變。我們提出了 SLeDGe，一種針對數據流的 SSL 方法，該方法在嚴格的記憶和標籤限制下共同學習預測模型和自適應圖結構。SLeDGe 使用不同的更新策略維護緊湊的標記和未標記記憶，在快速適應新特徵與保持歷史一致性之間取得平衡。此外，通過鼓勵關係圖的稀疏性，SLeDGe 過濾掉虛假的連接，並促進標籤監督的有效傳播。在 12 個數據集上，SLeDGe 超越了最先進的競爭對手，實現了在 0.1% 標籤下平均相對準確度提升 31.7%，在 1% 標籤下提升 14.8%。

##### **Coherence Under Commitment: Probing Generalization and Vacuous Memorization in LLM Logical Reasoning**
2606.21083v1 by Noor Islam S. Mohammad, Mahmudul Hasan

Large language models (LLMs) deployed for logical reasoning in knowledge-intensive domains exhibit a subtle but critical failure: coherence can be vacuously achieved through systematic abstention. A model that withholds commitment to either entailment or refutation satisfies negation consistency while providing no utility. We introduce Coherence Under Commitment (CUC), a dual-query evaluation paradigm that jointly measures consistency and decisiveness. CUC contributes three innovations: (1) a commitment score $c(\varphi) = p(\varphi) + p(\lnot\varphi)$ quantifying probability mass allocated to decisive outcomes; (2) a \textbf{deterministic elicitation protocol} via normalized YES/NO log probabilities, eliminating sampling variance; and (3) a 3-way decision framework (True/False/Uncertain) operationalizing the coherence-commitment trade-off into metrics. Experiments on four open-weight LLMs (1B-3B) across 204 FOLIO examples expose a sharp frontier. Qwen2.5-3B achieves near-zero contradiction ($\mathbb{E}[v_{\mathrm{neg}}]{=}0.025$) but only $7.4\%$ coverage, while TinyLlama-1.1B reaches $79.4\%$ coverage with violations on every example. Coherence-only evaluation would rank the abstaining model first; CUC exposes this as vacuous, and the frontier generalizes to LogiQA~v2 ($ρ{=}0.97$). We argue that evaluation must report both coherence and non-vacuous commitment and release a toolkit for standardized assessment.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在知識密集型領域中進行邏輯推理時，表現出一種微妙但關鍵的失敗：通過系統性的避免承諾可以虛無地實現一致性。一個對於推論或反駁都不作承諾的模型滿足否定一致性，但卻沒有提供任何效用。我們引入了承諾下的一致性（Coherence Under Commitment, CUC），這是一種雙查詢評估範式，聯合測量一致性和果斷性。CUC 貢獻了三項創新：（1）一個承諾分數 $c(\varphi) = p(\varphi) + p(\lnot\varphi)$，量化分配給果斷結果的概率質量；（2）通過標準化的 YES/NO 日誌概率的 \textbf{確定性引導協議}，消除抽樣變異；以及（3）一個三向決策框架（真/假/不確定），將一致性與承諾的權衡操作化為指標。在 204 個 FOLIO 範例上對四個開放權重的 LLM（1B-3B）進行的實驗顯示出一個明確的邊界。Qwen2.5-3B 實現了近零矛盾（$\mathbb{E}[v_{\mathrm{neg}}]{=}0.025$），但僅有 $7.4\%$ 的覆蓋率，而 TinyLlama-1.1B 則達到 $79.4\%$ 的覆蓋率，但每個範例都有違規。僅以一致性進行評估將使得避免承諾的模型排名第一；CUC 揭示了這一點是虛無的，並且邊界推廣到 LogiQA~v2 ($ρ{=}0.97$)。我們主張評估必須報告一致性和非虛無的承諾，並發布一個標準化評估的工具包。

##### **Local LLM Agents as Vulnerable Runtimes:A Source-Code Audit of the Agent Runtime Layer**
2606.21071v1 by Zhengsong Zhang, Zongze Li, Jiawei Guo, Haipeng Cai

Local LLM agents such as OpenClaw and Nanobot run on end-user machines and act on host resources - the shell, filesystem, browser, stored credentials, and messaging applications - through natural-language goals. These agents have become privileged software runtimes that mediate between user intent, model outputs, and host-level actions. Existing research characterizes the landscape through prompt injection, malicious skills, marketplace risks, or black-box evaluation of agents. But the implementation layer that performs this mediation, the prompt builder, parser, tool dispatcher, skill loader, memory writer, network client, and permission gate, has remained an unexamined safety boundary. To our knowledge, no prior work has examined the agent's source tree to audit these components for implementation-level security weaknesses. We present CLAWAUDIT, a static auditing framework for measuring vulnerability exposure in local LLM agent runtimes. CLAWAUDIT derives a five-category vulnerability taxonomy from STRIDE and develops custom static-analysis rules that target agent-specific patterns absent from established rule sets for vulnerability analysis. We instantiate the taxonomy in two backends, 47 Semgrep YAML rules and 30 CodeQL queries, and evaluate on OPENCLAWBENCH, a benchmark of 446 source-code-level advisories from the OpenClaw repository and split temporally into 229 rule-derivation (train) and 217 held-out (test) advisories. On the held-out test, CLAWAUDIT raises Semgrep recall from 21.7% (Pro baseline) to 66.8%, and CodeQL recall from 13.8% (security-extended) to 75.1%. Train/test gaps remain within 4 percentage points for all four configurations, indicating that the rules generalize to vulnerabilities unseen during rule writing. A preliminary live-code audit shows that these recall-oriented rules require manual triage, motivating semantic filtering before production deployment.

摘要：當地的 LLM 代理，例如 OpenClaw 和 Nanobot，運行在終端用戶的機器上，並通過自然語言目標作用於主機資源——外殼、檔案系統、瀏覽器、儲存的憑證和消息應用程序。這些代理已成為特權軟體運行時，調解用戶意圖、模型輸出和主機級行動之間的關係。現有研究通過提示注入、惡意技能、市場風險或代理的黑箱評估來描述這一領域。但執行這一調解的實施層，即提示生成器、解析器、工具調度器、技能加載器、記憶寫入器、網絡客戶端和權限閘，仍然是一個未經檢查的安全邊界。據我們所知，之前的工作尚未檢查代理的源樹，以審計這些組件的實施級安全弱點。我們提出了 CLAWAUDIT，一個靜態審計框架，用於測量本地 LLM 代理運行時的漏洞暴露。CLAWAUDIT 從 STRIDE 衍生出五類漏洞分類法，並開發針對代理特定模式的自定義靜態分析規則，這些模式在現有的漏洞分析規則集中缺失。我們在兩個後端中實例化了這一分類法，47 個 Semgrep YAML 規則和 30 個 CodeQL 查詢，並在 OPENCLAWBENCH 上進行評估，該基準來自 OpenClaw 存儲庫的 446 個源代碼級建議，並在時間上分為 229 個規則推導（訓練）和 217 個保留（測試）建議。在保留測試中，CLAWAUDIT 將 Semgrep 的召回率從 21.7%（Pro 基準）提高到 66.8%，將 CodeQL 的召回率從 13.8%（安全擴展）提高到 75.1%。所有四種配置的訓練/測試差距保持在 4 個百分點以內，這表明這些規則可以推廣到在規則編寫期間未見的漏洞。一項初步的實時代碼審計顯示，這些以召回為導向的規則需要手動分流，這促使在生產部署之前進行語義過濾。

##### **Negative Knowledge as Failure-aware Shared Memory for AutoResearch**
2606.21024v1 by Hanchun Wang

AI-assisted research systems generate many failed attempts, but those failures rarely become a durable, shared knowledge asset. We propose a negative knowledge memory layer: a curator agent converts each failed attempt into a bounded, typed record in a shared bank, and a downstream research agent explicitly adopts or rejects those records before proposing its next experiment. We evaluate this layer in two settings: same-task retry on ScienceAgentBench and cross-task scientific research on two nonlinear math-physics PDE problems. The negative knowledge layer outperforms vanilla AutoResearch baselines while using fewer tokens; agents with the negative knowledge bank solve new tasks that all baselines fail to solve in PDE systems research. We also show that the previous negative knowledge bank can transfer and enhance AutoResearch on different PDE problems. These results suggest that structured negative knowledge is a knowledge asset that should be explicitly maintained in broader AI-engaged scientific research beyond a memory-compression or debugging aid, alongside positive findings, as a collective infrastructure for scientific memory. Code is available at https://github.com/hch-wang/Negative_Knowledge.

摘要：AI輔助研究系統產生了許多失敗的嘗試，但這些失敗很少成為持久的共享知識資產。<lb/>我們提出了一個負知識記憶層：一個策展代理將每個失敗的嘗試轉換為共享庫中的有界類型記錄，而下游研究代理在提出下一個實驗之前明確地採納或拒絕這些記錄。<lb/>我們在兩個環境中評估這一層：在ScienceAgentBench上的同任務重試和在兩個非線性數學-物理PDE問題上的跨任務科學研究。<lb/>負知識層在使用更少的標記的同時，超越了普通AutoResearch基準；擁有負知識庫的代理能夠解決所有基準在PDE系統研究中無法解決的新任務。<lb/>我們還顯示，之前的負知識庫可以轉移並增強AutoResearch在不同PDE問題上的表現。<lb/>這些結果表明，結構化的負知識是一種應該在更廣泛的AI參與科學研究中明確維護的知識資產，除了作為記憶壓縮或調試輔助工具外，還應與正面發現一起作為科學記憶的集體基礎設施。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/hch-wang/Negative_Knowledge 獲得。

##### **Structure-Aware Graph Multi-Task Learning for Dynamic Sparse OD Demand Prediction**
2606.21022v1 by Ming Xu, Jiawei Cao

Origin-Destination (OD) demand prediction is fundamental to intelligent transportation systems, yet real-world OD flows are often dynamically sparse, long-tailed, and characterized by heterogeneous zero-flow patterns. These properties make it difficult to distinguish whether an OD connection is active from how much demand it generates once activated. Many existing methods primarily treat OD prediction as a single flow regression task, which limits their ability to model low-frequency, intermittent, and long-tailed OD interactions. To address these challenges, we propose SAGMTL, a Structure-Aware Graph Multi-Task Learning framework for dynamic sparse OD demand prediction. SAGMTL decomposes OD prediction into structural state modeling and flow intensity estimation, jointly learning regional activity states, OD connection activity, and edge-level flow intensity within a unified framework. Specifically, a node-edge collaborative representation module captures regional semantics, temporal dynamics, and spatial priors through interactive node-edge updates, producing structure-aware representations for dynamic OD interactions. Based on these representations, SAGMTL estimates OD flows by jointly modeling stable demand patterns and short-term fluctuations. A multi-constraint objective further improves sparsity awareness and structural consistency. Experiments on three real-world urban mobility datasets from Beijing, Chengdu, and Nanjing show that SAGMTL achieves superior overall performance compared with state-of-the-art baselines. Further analysis demonstrates that explicitly modeling regional activity, connection states, and flow intensity improves the robustness of dynamic sparse OD demand prediction.

摘要：Origin-Destination (OD) 需求預測是智能交通系統的基礎，然而現實世界中的 OD 流量通常是動態稀疏的、長尾的，並且特徵為異質的零流模式。<lb/>這些特性使得難以區分一個 OD 連接是否活躍，以及一旦啟動後它產生的需求量。<lb/>許多現有的方法主要將 OD 預測視為單一流量回歸任務，這限制了它們建模低頻、間歇性和長尾 OD 互動的能力。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了 SAGMTL，一個結構感知的圖形多任務學習框架，用於動態稀疏的 OD 需求預測。<lb/>SAGMTL 將 OD 預測分解為結構狀態建模和流量強度估計，並在統一框架內共同學習區域活動狀態、OD 連接活動和邊緣級流量強度。<lb/>具體而言，一個節點-邊緣協作表示模塊通過互動的節點-邊緣更新捕捉區域語義、時間動態和空間先驗，為動態 OD 互動生成結構感知的表示。<lb/>基於這些表示，SAGMTL 通過共同建模穩定的需求模式和短期波動來估計 OD 流量。<lb/>一個多約束目標進一步提高了稀疏性意識和結構一致性。<lb/>在來自北京、成都和南京的三個現實世界城市出行數據集上的實驗表明，SAGMTL 相較於最先進的基準方法實現了更優的整體性能。<lb/>進一步的分析顯示，明確建模區域活動、連接狀態和流量強度提高了動態稀疏 OD 需求預測的穩健性。

##### **The Metanym Game: A Self-Contained, Self-Consistent LLM Peer-Community Benchmark for Structural Intelligence**
2606.21008v1 by David Nordfors

The metanym game is a competitive word game for LLMs that measures structural intelligence against established cognitive-science constructs. No content is given in advance; the contestants create all of it -- a new kind of analogy test, analogical production falsifiable sentence by sentence, with no fixed test set to leak into training (contamination-resistant by construction). In the council-of-peers benchmark, the contestants also rate each other's creations. We introduce the first spectral solution, to our knowledge, to the wicked problem of benchmarking LLMs' factual accuracy without golden keys or oracle models: one singular value decomposition of the evaluators' ratings matrix yields their competence as both generators and judges of true statements at once. Competence on the subjective criteria comes from each judge's rating consistency as the yardstick shifts. The factual rating correlates with GPQA Diamond at Pearson r = 0.92. Scored separately, making and judging dissociate -- judging is the scarcer skill: the strongest generators are middling judges, the sharpest judge a mid-pack generator. To scale, the strongest players form a council that does the official benchmarking; its seats are contestable -- a stronger model earns one on the benchmark's own rating. The benchmark is entirely self-contained and self-consistent, a stable gauge over time.

摘要：競爭性字詞遊戲是針對大型語言模型（LLMs）的競爭性遊戲，測量結構智慧與既定的認知科學構造。沒有提前提供任何內容；參賽者創造所有內容——這是一種新的類比測試，類比產出逐句可證偽，沒有固定的測試集會洩漏到訓練中（從結構上抵抗污染）。在同儕評議的基準中，參賽者也會評價彼此的創作。我們介紹了第一個譜解決方案，據我們所知，針對評估LLMs事實準確性的棘手問題，無需黃金鑰匙或神諭模型：評估者評分矩陣的一次奇異值分解同時產生他們作為真實陳述的生成者和評判者的能力。對主觀標準的能力來自於每位評判的評分一致性，因為標準在變化。事實評分與GPQA Diamond的皮爾遜相關係數r = 0.92相關。分開計分時，創作和評判是分開的——評判是更稀缺的技能：最強的生成者是中等的評判者，而最敏銳的評判者則是中等的生成者。為了擴展，最強的參賽者組成一個理事會，負責官方基準測試；其席位是可競爭的——更強的模型在基準的自身評分中獲得席位。該基準完全自包含且自洽，隨時間穩定。

##### **Text-to-Image Generative AI for Modeling and Simulation: Methods, Opportunities, and Applications**
2606.20991v1 by Philippe J. Giabbanelli

Text-to-image generation is a form of generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) that converts textual descriptions into images. Most applications of GenAI in modeling and simulation (M&S) have focused on large language models for documentation, coding, or explanation. By contrast, the potential of image generation remains largely unexplored. This tutorial introduces text-to-image generation to the M&S community and details how it can support several M&S tasks, including communicating conceptual models, visualizing simulation outcomes, generating educational materials, and interfacing heterogeneous models in multi-scale simulations. The tutorial combines conceptual guidance with practical workflows, explaining how modern image generators operate, how prompts and simulation outputs can be translated into visual scenes, and how practitioners can integrate these tools into reproducible local pipelines. By focusing on transferable principles rather than specific tools, the tutorial equips M&S practitioners with the knowledge needed to evaluate, adopt, and adapt text-to-image generation in their simulation workflows.

摘要：文本到圖像生成是一種生成性人工智慧（GenAI），它將文本描述轉換為圖像。大多數GenAI在建模和模擬（M&S）中的應用主要集中在大型語言模型上，用於文檔、編碼或解釋。相比之下，圖像生成的潛力仍然大部分未被探索。這個教程向M&S社群介紹文本到圖像生成，並詳細說明它如何支持幾個M&S任務，包括傳達概念模型、可視化模擬結果、生成教育材料，以及在多尺度模擬中接口異構模型。這個教程結合了概念指導和實際工作流程，解釋了現代圖像生成器如何運作，提示和模擬輸出如何轉換為視覺場景，以及從業者如何將這些工具整合到可重複的本地流程中。通過專注於可轉移的原則而不是特定工具，這個教程為M&S從業者提供了評估、採用和調整文本到圖像生成在其模擬工作流程中所需的知識。

##### **How Should Agents Read Demonstrations? Hierarchical Structure Beats Flat Action Logs**
2606.20978v1 by Honjar Xing, Jefferson Lin, Henry Lieberman

Programming by Demonstration (PbD) offers a human-centered way to author procedural knowledge for LLM agents: users communicate what they want by showing rather than by writing prompts or code, making agent authoring accessible to non-programmers. The natural output of a PbD recording is a flat action log, but how this log is organized before being passed to the agent is an open design question with significant consequences for plan quality. We propose grouping recorded actions into labeled, hierarchical subgoals and evaluate the effect of this organizational structure in a controlled experiment. Across 85 web automation tasks, we compare a zero-shot baseline against four demonstration formats that share identical action sequences but differ in structure. On 43 natural-language tasks with vague descriptions, hierarchically grouped demonstrations improve pass rates from 76.7\% to 90.7\% (paired permutation test $p{=}0.034$; win-loss 6:0), while flat demonstrations show a smaller, non-significant improvement. On 42 tasks with precise descriptions, no format provides any benefit, confirming that the hierarchical advantage arises specifically when descriptions leave procedural details ambiguous. Ablation shows that subgoal grouping alone drives the effect: preconditions, postconditions, and parameter annotations add no measurable benefit. These results offer a concrete design recommendation for PbD pipelines and, more broadly, for any system that feeds procedural context to an LLM agent: segment action sequences into named subgoal groups rather than presenting flat step lists.

摘要：程式設計示範（PbD）提供了一種以人為中心的方法來為大型語言模型（LLM）代理編寫程序知識：用戶通過展示而不是編寫提示或代碼來表達他們的需求，使得代理編寫對非程序員來說變得可及。PbD 錄製的自然輸出是一個扁平的行動日誌，但在傳遞給代理之前，這個日誌的組織方式是一個開放的設計問題，對計劃質量有重大影響。我們提議將錄製的行動分組為標記的層次子目標，並在一個控制實驗中評估這種組織結構的效果。在 85 個網頁自動化任務中，我們將零樣本基準與四種示範格式進行比較，這些格式共享相同的行動序列，但結構不同。在 43 個具有模糊描述的自然語言任務中，層次分組的示範將通過率從 76.7\% 提高到 90.7\%（配對置換檢驗 $p{=}0.034$；勝負比 6:0），而扁平示範的改善則較小且不具顯著性。在 42 個具有精確描述的任務中，沒有任何格式提供任何好處，確認層次優勢特別出現在描述留下程序細節模糊的情況下。消融實驗顯示，僅僅是子目標分組驅動了這一效果：前置條件、後置條件和參數註釋沒有帶來可測量的好處。這些結果為 PbD 管道提供了一個具體的設計建議，更廣泛地說，對於任何將程序上下文提供給 LLM 代理的系統：將行動序列劃分為命名的子目標組，而不是呈現扁平的步驟列表。

##### **AutoACSL: Synthesizing ACSL Specifications by Integrating LLMs with CPG-Based Static Analysis**
2606.20969v1 by Han Zhou, Yu Luo, Dianxiang Xu

Generating formal specifications for C programs remains a challenge in formal verification due to the manual effort, expertise, and semantic precision required. While recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) offer promise in automating specification synthesis, current approaches often lack semantic depth and produce unverifiable or incomplete contracts. To address these limitations, we introduce AutoACSL, a novel framework that integrates LLM prompting with semantic features extracted from Code Property Graphs (CPGs). AutoACSL performs static analyses to extract key semantic elements, including arithmetic operations, loop and recursion structures, and return value propagation, which are encoded into structured prompts. These prompts enable the LLM not only to generate normal behavioral specifications but also to include constraints that prevent inputs leading to runtime errors. AutoACSL employs a feedback-driven synthesis loop, where candidate specifications are verified using Frama-C/WP and refined iteratively until verification succeeds or a termination condition is met. Evaluated on 604 programs drawn from diverse datasets, AutoACSL achieves a 98% specification generation success ratio and a 96% full proof ratio when paired with Gemini-3. Compared to a code-only baseline, AutoACSL improves the full proof ratio by 24.7% to 51.7% across four LLMs (GPT-o4 Mini, GPT-5.2, Grok-4.1, and Gemini-3), demonstrating that integrating large language models with CPG-based static analysis substantially enhances both generation robustness and verification effectiveness for automated ACSL specification synthesis.

摘要：生成 C 程式的正式規範在形式驗證中仍然是一個挑戰，因為這需要手動努力、專業知識和語義精確性。雖然最近在大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的進展提供了自動化規範合成的希望，但當前的方法往往缺乏語義深度，並產生不可驗證或不完整的合約。為了解決這些限制，我們介紹了 AutoACSL，一個新穎的框架，將 LLM 提示與從代碼屬性圖（CPGs）中提取的語義特徵相結合。AutoACSL 執行靜態分析以提取關鍵語義元素，包括算術運算、迴圈和遞歸結構以及返回值傳播，這些元素被編碼為結構化提示。這些提示使 LLM 不僅能生成正常行為的規範，還能包含防止導致運行時錯誤的輸入的約束。AutoACSL 採用反饋驅動的合成迴圈，候選規範通過 Frama-C/WP 進行驗證，並迭代地進行精煉，直到驗證成功或滿足終止條件。根據來自多樣數據集的 604 程式進行評估，AutoACSL 在與 Gemini-3 配對時達到了 98% 的規範生成成功率和 96% 的完整證明率。與僅基於代碼的基準相比，AutoACSL 在四個 LLM（GPT-o4 Mini、GPT-5.2、Grok-4.1 和 Gemini-3）中將完整證明率提高了 24.7% 至 51.7%，顯示出將大型語言模型與基於 CPG 的靜態分析相結合，顯著增強了自動化 ACSL 規範合成的生成穩健性和驗證有效性。

##### **Right Knowledge, Wrong Answer: Test-Time Steering for Temporal Fact Conflicts in Open-Weight Language Models**
2606.20959v1 by Elias Hossain, Sourav Saha, Umesh Chandra Biswas, Sanjeda Sara Jennifer

Large language models can store both outdated facts and newer superseding facts in their parameters, but standard prompting may still elicit the outdated answer. We formalize this problem as Parametric Temporal Conflict (PTC) and introduce Temporal Attractor Steering (TAS), a three-stage test-time intervention that detects likely conflicts, identifies a conflict-critical layer, and steers hidden states toward newer-fact representations without retraining or external retrieval. We construct an 8,746-record verified benchmark across five Wikidata relations and evaluate four open-weight language models from three families: Qwen-2.5-1.5B/7B, Mistral-7B-v0.3, and Llama-3.1-8B. Single-layer activation patching achieves answer-flip rates of 0.72-0.85 across all models. End-to-end TAS resolves 29-57% of PTC cases while preserving 85-99% accuracy on non-conflict queries, outperforming a matched ITI baseline on three of four models. These results show that outdated parametric knowledge can be selectively overridden at inference time.

摘要：大型語言模型可以在其參數中存儲過時的事實和更新的取代事實，但標準提示仍可能引出過時的答案。我們將這個問題形式化為參數時間衝突（PTC），並引入時間吸引器引導（TAS），這是一種三階段的測試時間干預，能夠檢測可能的衝突，識別衝突關鍵層，並在不重新訓練或外部檢索的情況下，將隱藏狀態引導至更新事實的表示。我們構建了一個包含8,746條記錄的經過驗證的基準，涵蓋五個Wikidata關係，並評估來自三個家族的四個開放權重語言模型：Qwen-2.5-1.5B/7B、Mistral-7B-v0.3和Llama-3.1-8B。單層激活修補在所有模型中實現了0.72-0.85的答案翻轉率。端到端的TAS解決了29-57%的PTC案例，同時在非衝突查詢上保持了85-99%的準確率，並在四個模型中的三個上超越了匹配的ITI基線。這些結果表明，過時的參數知識可以在推理時被選擇性地覆蓋。

##### **Scaling Diverse Language Generation for 3D Visual Grounding**
2606.20946v1 by Austin T. Wang, Dongchen Yang, Angel X. Chang

Developing robust models for 3D visual grounding (3DVG), the localization of entities in a 3D scene described in natural language, is important for enabling agents to correspond spatial language with objects in the physical world. However, the lack of diverse descriptions at scale prevents models from generalizing beyond simple linguistic patterns. Recent such attempts lack diversity in the constraint types and language used to ground objects. Captioning methods cannot precisely contrast objects, which is important for visual grounding. We therefore propose ViGiL3D++, a scalable, scene-agnostic method that generates diverse visual grounding queries by combining constraint sampling in scene graphs with the language generation of LLMs. We show that it has greater diversity over existing scaled datasets and improves model performance over several 3DVG benchmarks but also illuminates outstanding limitations of VLMs.

摘要：開發穩健的3D視覺定位模型（3DVG），即在自然語言中描述的3D場景中定位實體，對於使代理能夠將空間語言與物理世界中的物體相對應至關重要。<lb/>然而，缺乏多樣化的描述使得模型無法超越簡單的語言模式進行泛化。<lb/>最近的此類嘗試在約束類型和用於定位物體的語言上缺乏多樣性。<lb/>標題生成方法無法精確對比物體，而這對於視覺定位非常重要。<lb/>因此，我們提出了ViGiL3D++，這是一種可擴展的、場景無關的方法，通過將場景圖中的約束採樣與大型語言模型的語言生成相結合，生成多樣化的視覺定位查詢。<lb/>我們顯示它在現有的擴展數據集上具有更大的多樣性，並在幾個3DVG基準上提高了模型性能，但也揭示了VLMs的顯著限制。

##### **Root Cause Analysis with Latent Confounders using Partial Ancestral Graphs**
2606.20912v1 by Henrique O. Caetano, Rafael Arone, Carlos Dias Maciel

Finding the source of failures, known as Root Cause Analysis (RCA), is essential for identifying the root causes of anomalies and maintaining the reliability of complex systems. While causal theory has advanced data-driven RCA, existing frameworks assume causal sufficiency, failing to account for the unobserved latent variables prevalent in real-world environments. To address this gap, we propose PAG-RCA. This framework models system failures as parametric interventions over Partial Ancestral Graphs (PAGs) to perform RCA in the presence of latent variables. We use standard causal identification algorithms to find the source of failures by quantifying causal effects over the PAG. When an effect is identifiable, candidate root causes are ranked based on their exact intervention effects. When effects are structurally unidentifiable, our framework (for the first time in the RCA literature) integrates partial identification to evaluate and score candidates using analytical causal bounds. By integrating latent variables and partial identification at once our framework ensures robust RCA even under data scarcity and latent-variable scenarios where traditional methods degrade. Evaluations on synthetic data, microservice anomaly benchmarks and power-grid cascading failures demonstrate that PAG-RCA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art data-driven baselines. By improving data-driven RCA performance under data scarcity, this methodology advances reliable automated diagnostics in partially observable complex networks.

摘要：尋找失敗的根源，被稱為根本原因分析（Root Cause Analysis, RCA），對於識別異常的根本原因和維護複雜系統的可靠性至關重要。雖然因果理論已經推進了數據驅動的 RCA，但現有框架假設因果充分性，未能考慮在現實環境中普遍存在的未觀察潛在變量。為了解決這一問題，我們提出了 PAG-RCA。該框架將系統失敗建模為在部分祖先圖（Partial Ancestral Graphs, PAGs）上的參數干預，以便在存在潛在變量的情況下執行 RCA。我們使用標準因果識別算法通過量化 PAG 上的因果效應來找出失敗的根源。當一個效應是可識別的時候，候選根本原因根據其確切的干預效應進行排名。當效應在結構上不可識別時，我們的框架（在 RCA 文獻中首次）整合了部分識別，使用分析性因果界限來評估和打分候選者。通過同時整合潛在變量和部分識別，我們的框架確保了即使在數據稀缺和潛在變量情境下，RCA 也能保持穩健性，而傳統方法在這些情況下會退化。在合成數據、微服務異常基準和電力網絡級聯故障的評估中，PAG-RCA 始終優於最先進的數據驅動基準。通過改善在數據稀缺下的數據驅動 RCA 性能，這種方法推進了在部分可觀察複雜網絡中可靠的自動診斷。

##### **The Token Tax of Epistemic Accuracy: Comparing RAG and Long-Context Architectures for Document-Grounded Generative AI Applications**
2606.20898v1 by Austin Hamilton, Ryan Singh, Michael Wise, Ibrahim Yousif, Arthur Carvalho, Zhe Shan, Mohammad Mayyas, Lora A. Cavuoto, Fadel M. Megahed

Document-grounded assistants built on large language models are increasingly used in high-stakes, knowledge-intensive work. Their usefulness, however, may depend on how evidence is allocated before generation. We investigate such a claim by comparing two grounding architectures: (a) retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) that retrieves a few relevant passages, and (b) long-context prompting, which loads the whole document collection in context. We view these as two regimes of "epistemic access" on an accuracy--cost frontier. We use "epistemic accuracy" to capture model correctness that depends on having the right evidence. We posit that broader access (via long context) can increase it, but with a "token tax" (i.e., a substantial increase in cost due to larger input token consumption). We probe this framing with a case study in manufacturing safety training. Using an expert-validated benchmark, we evaluate 972 answers across three machines, two small language models, and three retrieval/in-context prompting approaches. Long-context prompting achieved the highest correctness (73.1% vs. 65.4% for semantic RAG), but at 26 times the per-query token cost. We interpret this gap as the token tax of broader evidentiary access. We carefully discuss the implications of our findings for resource-constrained organizations.

摘要：基於大型語言模型的文件基礎助手在高風險、知識密集的工作中越來越受到使用。 然而，它們的有效性可能取決於生成前證據的分配方式。 我們通過比較兩種基礎架構來調查這一主張：(a) 檢索增強生成（RAG），它檢索幾個相關段落，以及 (b) 長上下文提示，該方法將整個文檔集合加載到上下文中。 我們將這兩者視為“認識論訪問”在準確性—成本邊界上的兩種模式。 我們使用“認識論準確性”來捕捉模型正確性，這取決於擁有正確的證據。 我們假設更廣泛的訪問（通過長上下文）可以提高準確性，但會產生“令牌稅”（即，由於更大的輸入令牌消耗而導致成本的顯著增加）。 我們通過製造安全培訓的案例研究來探討這一框架。 使用專家驗證的基準，我們評估了三台機器、兩個小型語言模型和三種檢索/上下文提示方法的972個答案。 長上下文提示達到了最高的正確性（73.1% 對比語義 RAG 的 65.4%），但每查詢的令牌成本為26倍。 我們將這一差距解釋為更廣泛證據訪問的令牌稅。 我們仔細討論了我們的發現對資源有限的組織的影響。

##### **Neurosymbolic Clinical Trial Matching via LLM-Driven Abduction and Logical Verification**
2606.20895v1 by Baiyang Qu, Leonardo Ranaldi, Xi Wang, Marco Valentino

Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising path to automate Clinical Trial Matching (CTM), but still struggle with the deterministic verification required for complex eligibility criteria. Conversely, purely symbolic methods provide formal rigour but break down when faced with incomplete patient records and noisy clinical evidence. To bridge this gap, we investigate a hybrid framework for CTM combining LLMs with logical verification. In particular, we introduce an abductive neurosymbolic CTM framework (αNeSy-CTM), which leverages the linguistic and world knowledge in LLMs to support reasoning over noisy and underspecified clinical text. Extensive evaluation demonstrates that αNeSy-CTM substantially outperforms standalone LLM baselines, achieving up to 30% relative improvement over zero-shot baselines. In addition, our analyses confirm the impact of abductive reasoning on CTM, with αNeSy-CTM exhibiting improved accuracy, specificity, and robustness over a non-abductive neurosymbolic setting. Furthermore, αNeSy-CTM and Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning prove highly complementary, highlighting the potential for a hybrid routing policy. Ultimately, this paper demonstrates the impact of neurosymbolic methods for automating CTM, providing a path toward the next generation of auditable, LLM-driven clinical applications.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）為自動化臨床試驗匹配（CTM）提供了一條有希望的途徑，但在處理複雜的資格標準所需的確定性驗證時仍然面臨挑戰。相反，純符號方法提供了形式上的嚴謹性，但在面對不完整的病歷和嘈雜的臨床證據時會崩潰。為了彌補這一差距，我們研究了一個結合LLMs與邏輯驗證的CTM混合框架。特別是，我們介紹了一個推理神經符號CTM框架（αNeSy-CTM），該框架利用LLMs中的語言和世界知識來支持對嘈雜和不明確的臨床文本進行推理。廣泛的評估顯示，αNeSy-CTM的表現顯著優於獨立的LLM基準，實現了相對於零樣本基準高達30%的改進。此外，我們的分析確認了推理對CTM的影響，αNeSy-CTM在準確性、特異性和穩健性方面優於非推理神經符號設置。此外，αNeSy-CTM和思維鏈（CoT）推理被證明是高度互補的，突顯了混合路由策略的潛力。最終，本文展示了神經符號方法在自動化CTM中的影響，為下一代可審核的、以LLM驅動的臨床應用提供了道路。

##### **The Substrate Collapse: AI Code Generation Invalidates Authorship-Based Knowledge Metrics**
2606.20882v1 by Brett Wheeler

Software engineering has long inferred where a system's knowledge resides from who authored its code. The truck factor, the Degree-of-Authorship metric, and the degree-of-knowledge model all rest on one inference -- that authoring a region of code is evidence of understanding it -- and for most of software's history it was a workable proxy, because code entered a repository only when a human wrote it, which forced at least transient understanding. This paper argues that AI code generation severs that inference at its root, and that the consequence is not the degradation of the authorship-based metrics but their invalidation as a class. When an agent generates a module and a human merges it, the version-control record still attributes authorship, but the attribution no longer licenses any conclusion about comprehension: the same footprint is now compatible with full, partial, or no understanding. The metric still returns a number; the number measures a substrate that has come uncoupled from the quantity it was used to estimate. The collapse is corroborated by the field's own measurement failures, and the methodological corollary is load-bearing: the instrument the comprehension-debt era needs cannot be built by refining the knowledge-concentration metrics, because no function of an authorship footprint recovers an inference the footprint no longer supports. The replacement must be grounded in evidence of comprehension rather than authorship. I state a falsifiable prediction that discriminates the two -- that systems with a healthy authorship-derived truck factor but low comprehension-measured retention will suffer incident-resolution failures the authorship metric does not predict -- and argue that building the comprehension-grounded instrument at the scale of a system and a team is the field's open measurement problem, left open here.

摘要：軟體工程長期以來都是根據誰撰寫了代碼來推斷系統的知識所在。卡車因子、作者度量標準和知識程度模型都基於一個推論——撰寫一段代碼是理解它的證據——在大多數軟體歷史中，這是一個可行的代理，因為代碼只有在被人類撰寫時才會進入倉庫，這至少強迫了短暫的理解。本文主張，AI代碼生成從根本上切斷了這一推論，其結果不是基於作者的度量標準的降級，而是作為一個類別的無效化。當一個代理生成一個模塊並且一個人類合併它時，版本控制記錄仍然歸屬於作者，但這種歸屬不再授權任何關於理解的結論：相同的足跡現在可以與完全、部分或沒有理解兼容。該度量仍然返回一個數字；這個數字測量的是一個已經與其用來估算的數量脫鉤的基底。這一崩潰得到了該領域自身測量失敗的證實，並且方法論的推論是承載性的：理解債務時代所需的工具無法通過精煉知識集中度量標準來構建，因為沒有任何基於作者足跡的函數能夠恢復一個該足跡不再支持的推論。替代品必須基於理解的證據，而不是作者身份。我提出一個可反駁的預測來區分這兩者——即擁有健康的基於作者的卡車因子但低理解測量保留的系統將遭受作者度量無法預測的事件解決失敗——並主張在系統和團隊的規模上構建基於理解的工具是該領域的開放測量問題，這裡仍然未解決。

##### **Can LLMs Reason About Brand Ownership? An Empirical Study of Domain Attribution Intelligence**
2606.20868v1 by Fathima Mashood, Mohamed Nabeel

When a new domain resembling a popular brand appears, defenders face a fundamental ambiguity: it may be an attacker-created squatting site for phishing, or it may be a domain the brand itself registered, either defensively, to block attackers, or legitimately, for a new product or service launch. Incorrectly flagging a brand-owned domain as malicious produces a false positive that harms end users and damages the brand's reputation. Resolving this ambiguity requires brand intelligence: the ability to determine, at scale, whether a given domain belongs to a brand. Large language models (LLMs), with their broad knowledge of brand domain relationships, offer a promising zero configuration approach to this problem, but their reliability for brand intelligence tasks remains unknown. We present the first systematic empirical evaluation of LLM brand intelligence across three tasks: domain enumeration (Q1), open ended brand attribution (Q2), and binary ownership classification (Q3). We evaluate four models, Gemini 2.5 Flash, Gemini 3.5 Flash, Claude Sonnet 4.5, and Claude Sonnet 4.6, across four retrieval settings (in context, web search, WHOIS lookup, and combined) on 36 of the most phished brands. Our results reveal a stark dichotomy: models achieve up to 82% precision enumerating brand domains from memory alone, yet fail at ownership verification without external tools, with macro F1 at most 0.37 in ICL mode. WHOIS augmentation lifts Q3 macro F1 by up to 0.65 points, yielding near perfect precision (<= 0.99), dramatically reducing the false positive risk for defenders. We provide concrete recommendations for deploying LLMs in brand protection pipelines.

摘要：當一個新的域名出現，類似於一個受歡迎的品牌時，防禦者面臨一個根本的模糊性：這可能是攻擊者創建的用於網絡釣魚的佔用網站，或者這可能是品牌本身註冊的域名，無論是出於防禦目的以阻止攻擊者，還是合法地為新產品或服務的推出。錯誤地將品牌擁有的域名標記為惡意會產生虛假正面，這會損害最終用戶並損害品牌的聲譽。解決這一模糊性需要品牌情報：能夠在大規模上確定給定域名是否屬於某個品牌的能力。大型語言模型（LLMs）憑藉其對品牌域名關係的廣泛知識，為這個問題提供了一種有前景的零配置方法，但它們在品牌情報任務中的可靠性仍然未知。我們對LLM品牌情報在三個任務上的首次系統實證評估進行了展示：域名枚舉（Q1）、開放式品牌歸屬（Q2）和二元所有權分類（Q3）。我們在36個最常被釣魚的品牌上，評估了四個模型，分別是Gemini 2.5 Flash、Gemini 3.5 Flash、Claude Sonnet 4.5和Claude Sonnet 4.6，在四種檢索設定（上下文、網絡搜索、WHOIS查詢和綜合）下進行評估。我們的結果揭示了一個明顯的二分法：模型在僅憑記憶枚舉品牌域名時達到最高82%的精確度，但在沒有外部工具的情況下無法進行所有權驗證，ICL模式下的宏觀F1最高為0.37。WHOIS增強將Q3的宏觀F1提升了最多0.65個點，實現了近乎完美的精確度（<= 0.99），顯著降低了防禦者的虛假正面風險。我們提供了具體的建議，用於在品牌保護管道中部署LLMs。

##### **Structuring and Tokenizing Distributed User Interest Context for Generative Recommendation**
2606.20554v1 by Ruizhong Qiu, Yinglong Xia, Dongqi Fu, Hanqing Zeng, Ren Chen, Xiangjun Fan, Hong Li, Hong Yan, Hanghang Tong

Generative recommendation is an emerging paradigm that has shown promise in industrial recommendation systems, aiming to predict users' next interactions from their historical behaviors. At the core of generative recommendation lies item tokenization, which bridges item semantics and recommendation models. However, existing methods often struggle to effectively organize and inject complex user-behavioral and item-semantic contexts into recommendation models simultaneously. On the one hand, existing graph-based integration methods, such as graph serialization and graph neural networks, either suffer from scalability issues or exploit only local graph information. On the other hand, existing semantic tokenization methods typically rely on heuristics and lack explicit supervision signals, which may lead to inaccurate or suboptimal semantic representations. To address these limitations in user interest context modeling, we propose G2Rec, a scalable framework that unifies holistic graph-based user co-engagement modeling with semantic tokenization for industrial-scale generative recommendation. Overall, G2Rec enables recommendation models to capture holistic and semantically grounded user interest prototypes without requiring ground-truth user interests, thereby providing more comprehensive and accurate modeling of user behavior contexts in industrial sequential recommendation. Online deployment across product surfaces and extensive experiments on public datasets demonstrate the superiority of G2Rec over existing methods.

摘要：生成推薦是一種新興的範式，已在工業推薦系統中顯示出潛力，旨在根據用戶的歷史行為預測其下一次互動。生成推薦的核心在於項目標記化，它橋接了項目語義和推薦模型。然而，現有的方法往往難以有效地組織和注入複雜的用戶行為和項目語義上下文到推薦模型中。 一方面，現有的基於圖的整合方法，如圖序列化和圖神經網絡，要麼面臨可擴展性問題，要麼僅利用局部圖信息。另一方面，現有的語義標記化方法通常依賴於啟發式，並缺乏明確的監督信號，這可能導致不準確或次優的語義表示。為了解決用戶興趣上下文建模中的這些限制，我們提出了G2Rec，一個可擴展的框架，將整體基於圖的用戶共同參與建模與語義標記化統一，用於工業規模的生成推薦。總體而言，G2Rec使推薦模型能夠捕捉整體和語義基礎的用戶興趣原型，而無需真實的用戶興趣，從而在工業序列推薦中提供更全面和準確的用戶行為上下文建模。跨產品表面的在線部署和在公共數據集上的廣泛實驗證明了G2Rec相對於現有方法的優越性。

##### **CATCH-ME if you RAG: a dataset of Contextually Annotated multi-Turn Counterspeech against Hate and Misinformation Exchanges**
2606.20369v1 by Helena Bonaldi, Genoveffa Martone, Marco Guerini

Online hate speech and misinformation frequently overlap, yet NLP research has mainly treated them in isolation. While LLMs represent a scalable solution for assisting humans in the generation of counterspeech for both threats, zero-shot models frequently generate repetitive and vague responses, underscoring the need for high-quality examples to steer model generation. However, existing counterspeech datasets against the overlap of hate and misinformation are scarce and limited to single-turn English dialogues, while real-life interactions span across multiple turns and languages. To bridge this gap, we introduce the first large-scale, expert-curated, multilingual dataset of dialogues tackling the intersection of hate and misinformation. To ensure factual grounding, the dialogues are also anchored in verified external knowledge (i.e., fact-checking articles and NGO reports) and include document- and chunk-level span annotations, making it directly applicable for RAG systems. 摘要：線上仇恨言論和錯誤資訊經常重疊，然而自然語言處理研究主要將它們孤立對待。雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）代表了一種可擴展的解決方案，幫助人類生成針對這兩種威脅的反駁言論，但零樣本模型經常生成重複且模糊的回應，突顯出需要高質量範例來引導模型生成。然而，現有針對仇恨和錯誤資訊重疊的反駁言論數據集稀缺，且僅限於單輪的英語對話，而現實生活中的互動則跨越多輪和多種語言。為了填補這一空白，我們介紹了第一個大規模、專家策劃的多語言對話數據集，專注於解決仇恨和錯誤資訊的交集。為了確保事實基礎，這些對話也基於經過驗證的外部知識（即事實查核文章和非政府組織報告），並包括文檔和片段級別的範圍標註，使其可直接應用於檢索增強生成（RAG）系統。這一新資源涵蓋五種語言，針對七個邊緣化群體的仇恨言論，使得訓練和評估更具說服力、事實基礎的反駁言論模型成為可能。

##### **Boundary Embedding Shaping with Adaptive Contrastive Learning for Graph Structural Disentanglement**
2606.20283v1 by Jiaqing Chen, Zidu Yin, Yichao Cai, Yuhang Liu, Zhen Zhang, Dong Gong, Javen Qinfeng Shi

Graph neural networks (GNNs) excel at aggregating neighbor information for classification, yet their performance is hindered by graph structural entanglement, where spurious correlations from semantically irrelevant neighbors contaminate node embeddings. This challenge is most acute for nodes near class boundaries in the embedding space, where amplified structural noise blurs decision boundaries and destabilizes predictions. Existing robust GNN methods largely treat all nodes uniformly, ignoring boundary vulnerabilities. In this paper, to improve classification performance, we tackle graph structural disentanglement by identifying boundary-region entanglement as the primary bottleneck and propose Boundary Embedding Shaping (BES), an adaptive contrastive learning GNN plug-in module that selectively suppresses spurious structural noise at decision boundaries with minimal model parameter perturbation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that BES consistently improves boundary discrimination and outperforms existing leading methods. Notably, BES boosts GCN performance by an average of 3.3% in node classification (up to 5.0% on WikiCS) and achieves superior accuracy in link prediction.

摘要：圖神經網絡（GNNs）在聚合鄰居信息以進行分類方面表現出色，但其性能受到圖結構糾纏的阻礙，這種情況下，來自語義上不相關鄰居的虛假相關性會污染節點嵌入。這一挑戰在嵌入空間中接近類別邊界的節點上最為明顯，增強的結構噪聲模糊了決策邊界並使預測不穩定。現有的穩健GNN方法大多將所有節點視為均勻，忽略了邊界的脆弱性。本文為了提高分類性能，通過將邊界區域糾纏識別為主要瓶頸，來解決圖結構解糾纏問題，並提出了邊界嵌入塑形（BES），這是一個自適應對比學習GNN插件模塊，能夠在決策邊界上選擇性地抑制虛假結構噪聲，並且對模型參數的擾動最小。大量實驗表明，BES持續改善邊界區分能力，並超越現有的領先方法。值得注意的是，BES在節點分類中平均提升了GCN性能3.3%（在WikiCS上最高可達5.0%），並在鏈接預測中實現了更高的準確性。

##### **Editorial Alignment: A Participatory Approach to Engaging Editorial Expertise in LLM-mediated Knowledge Dissemination**
2606.20258v1 by Simon Aagaard Enni, Malthe Stavning Erslev, Karl-Emil Kjær Bilstrup, Kristoffer Laigaard Nielbo

The emergence of LLM-driven information services is reshaping the conditions under which public knowledge institutions operate, threatening to absorb the editorial function these institutions exist to exercise. While LLMs offer powerful new affordances for knowledge dissemination, editorial authority is challenged by pretrained LLMs that arrive already aligned with the values and dissemination strategies of their commercial developers. This paper investigates editor participation in re-aligning LLM interfaces to editorial standards through design workshops, in a case study where we design and implement an LLM-enabled encyclopedia interface with a Nordic public knowledge institution. We introduce editorial alignment as a design practice within Participatory AI, framing AI alignment as a design process and positioning the editorial standard as a design artefact that translates editorial practice and values into alignment objectives for technical implementation. Last, we discuss how editorial alignment can create space for ongoing participation and give editors agency in LLM-mediated knowledge dissemination.

##### **Navigating Unreliable Parametric and Contextual Knowledge: Explicit Knowledge Conflict Resolution for LLM Inference**
2606.20245v1 by Huang Peng, Jiuyang Tang, Weixin Zeng, Hao Xu, Xiang Zhao

Large language models (LLMs) have achieved strong performance across a wide range of language-based tasks by leveraging both extensive parametric knowledge and in-context learning ability, enabling them to incorporate external information provided in the input prompt. However, the integration of external knowledge can introduce conflicts, not only between the model's internal parametric knowledge and the external information, but also among multiple pieces of external contexts. Existing approaches typically assume that either the model or the provided context is reliable, overlooking the possibility that both sources may contain errors, and avoid conflicts by privileging one source over the other, rather than actively resolving inconsistencies. To address these limitations, we propose a novel framework MACR for LLM knowledge conflict resolution that moves beyond the conventional binary choice paradigm and incorporates an explicit conflict-resolution mechanism based on a multi-agent reasoning approach. Specifically, we first propose an adaptive knowledge assessment and retrieval approach that employs a modified semantic entropy measure to quantify an LLM's confidence in its answer to a given query. Based on this confidence estimation, MACR either externalizes the model's internal knowledge as textual representations or retrieves relevant external knowledge when internal knowledge is insufficient, generating basic contexts for subsequent reasoning. Then we introduce an inductive multi-agent reasoning framework with three specialized agents that, respectively, induce explicit rules, analyze potential conflicts, and resolve inconsistencies across all available contexts. Empirical results demonstrate that MACR significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across benchmarks, while also providing interpretable resolutions of explicit conflicts.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）透過利用廣泛的參數知識和上下文學習能力，在各種基於語言的任務中取得了強勁的表現，使其能夠納入輸入提示中提供的外部信息。<lb/>然而，外部知識的整合可能會引入衝突，不僅在模型的內部參數知識與外部信息之間，還在多個外部上下文之間。<lb/>現有的方法通常假設模型或提供的上下文是可靠的，忽視了兩個來源都可能包含錯誤的可能性，並通過優先考慮一個來源而不是另一個來源來避免衝突，而不是主動解決不一致性。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了一個新框架 MACR，用於 LLM 知識衝突解決，超越傳統的二元選擇範式，並基於多代理推理方法納入明確的衝突解決機制。<lb/>具體而言，我們首先提出了一種自適應知識評估和檢索方法，該方法使用修改過的語義熵度量來量化 LLM 對給定查詢答案的信心。<lb/>根據這一信心評估，MACR 要麼將模型的內部知識外部化為文本表示，要麼在內部知識不足時檢索相關的外部知識，生成後續推理的基本上下文。<lb/>然後，我們引入了一個歸納多代理推理框架，該框架擁有三個專門的代理，分別引導明確規則、分析潛在衝突並解決所有可用上下文中的不一致性。<lb/>實證結果表明，MACR 在基準測試中顯著超越了最先進的基準，同時也提供了明確衝突的可解釋解決方案。
